\DoxyCodeLine{00041\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ in\ memory\ stack\ (0:default,\ fastest),\ or\ in\ memory\ heap\ (1:requires\ malloc()).}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00050\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00052\ \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00053\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ LZ4\_ACCELERATION\_MAX\ :}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00060\ \textcolor{comment}{/*-\/************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00061\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ CPU\ Feature\ Detection}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00062\ \textcolor{comment}{**************************************/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00063\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ LZ4\_FORCE\_MEMORY\_ACCESS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00064\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ By\ default,\ access\ to\ unaligned\ memory\ is\ controlled\ by\ \`{}memcpy()`,\ which\ is\ safe\ and\ portable.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00065\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Unfortunately,\ on\ some\ target/compiler\ combinations,\ the\ generated\ assembly\ is\ sub-\/optimal.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00066\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ The\ below\ switch\ allow\ to\ select\ different\ access\ method\ for\ improved\ performance.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00067\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Method\ 0\ (default)\ :\ use\ \`{}memcpy()`.\ Safe\ and\ portable.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00068\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Method\ 1\ :\ \`{}\_\_packed`\ statement.\ It\ depends\ on\ compiler\ extension\ (ie,\ not\ portable).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00069\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ This\ method\ is\ safe\ if\ your\ compiler\ supports\ it,\ and\ *generally*\ as\ fast\ or\ faster\ than\ \`{}memcpy`.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00070\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Method\ 2\ :\ direct\ access.\ This\ method\ is\ portable\ but\ violate\ C\ standard.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00071\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ It\ can\ generate\ buggy\ code\ on\ targets\ which\ assembly\ generation\ depends\ on\ alignment.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00072\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ But\ in\ some\ circumstances,\ it's\ the\ only\ known\ way\ to\ get\ the\ most\ performance\ (ie\ GCC\ +\ ARMv6)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00073\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ See\ https://fastcompression.blogspot.fr/2015/08/accessing-\/unaligned-\/memory.html\ for\ details.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00074\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Prefer\ these\ methods\ in\ priority\ order\ (0\ >\ 1\ >\ 2)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00075\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00076\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifndef\ LZ4\_FORCE\_MEMORY\_ACCESS\ \ \ }\textcolor{comment}{/*\ can\ be\ defined\ externally\ */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00077\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#\ \ if\ defined(\_\_GNUC\_\_)\ \&\&\ \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00078\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\ \ (\ defined(\_\_ARM\_ARCH\_6\_\_)\ ||\ defined(\_\_ARM\_ARCH\_6J\_\_)\ ||\ defined(\_\_ARM\_ARCH\_6K\_\_)\ \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00079\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\ \ ||\ defined(\_\_ARM\_ARCH\_6Z\_\_)\ ||\ defined(\_\_ARM\_ARCH\_6ZK\_\_)\ ||\ defined(\_\_ARM\_ARCH\_6T2\_\_)\ )}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00080\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#\ \ \ \ define\ LZ4\_FORCE\_MEMORY\_ACCESS\ 2}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00081\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#\ \ elif\ (defined(\_\_INTEL\_COMPILER)\ \&\&\ !defined(\_WIN32))\ ||\ defined(\_\_GNUC\_\_)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00082\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#\ \ \ \ define\ LZ4\_FORCE\_MEMORY\_ACCESS\ 1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00083\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#\ \ endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00084\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00085\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00086\ \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00087\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ LZ4\_FORCE\_SW\_BITCOUNT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00088\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Define\ this\ parameter\ if\ your\ target\ system\ or\ compiler\ does\ not\ support\ hardware\ bit\ count}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00089\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00090\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if\ defined(\_MSC\_VER)\ \&\&\ defined(\_WIN32\_WCE)\ \ \ }\textcolor{comment}{/*\ Visual\ Studio\ for\ WinCE\ doesn't\ support\ Hardware\ bit\ count\ */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00131\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#\ \ if\ defined\ (\_MSC\_VER)\ \&\&\ !defined\ (\_\_clang\_\_)\ \ \ \ }\textcolor{comment}{/*\ MSVC\ */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00132\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#\ \ \ \ define\ LZ4\_FORCE\_INLINE\ static\ \_\_forceinline}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00133\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#\ \ else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00134\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#\ \ \ \ if\ defined\ (\_\_cplusplus)\ ||\ defined\ (\_\_STDC\_VERSION\_\_)\ \&\&\ \_\_STDC\_VERSION\_\_\ >=\ 199901L\ \ \ }\textcolor{comment}{/*\ C99\ */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00137\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#\ \ \ \ \ \ else}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00140\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#\ \ \ \ else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00141\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#\ \ \ \ \ \ define\ LZ4\_FORCE\_INLINE\ static}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00142\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#\ \ \ \ endif\ }\textcolor{comment}{/*\ \_\_STDC\_VERSION\_\_\ */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00143\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#\ \ endif\ \ }\textcolor{comment}{/*\ \_MSC\_VER\ */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00144\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif\ }\textcolor{comment}{/*\ LZ4\_FORCE\_INLINE\ */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00145\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00146\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ LZ4\_FORCE\_O2\ and\ LZ4\_FORCE\_INLINE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00147\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ gcc\ on\ ppc64le\ generates\ an\ unrolled\ SIMDized\ loop\ for\ LZ4\_wildCopy8,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00148\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ together\ with\ a\ simple\ 8-\/byte\ copy\ loop\ as\ a\ fall-\/back\ path.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00149\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ However,\ this\ optimization\ hurts\ the\ decompression\ speed\ by\ >30\%,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00150\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ because\ the\ execution\ does\ not\ go\ to\ the\ optimized\ loop}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00151\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ for\ typical\ compressible\ data,\ and\ all\ of\ the\ preamble\ checks}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00152\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ before\ going\ to\ the\ fall-\/back\ path\ become\ useless\ overhead.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00153\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ This\ optimization\ happens\ only\ with\ the\ -\/O3\ flag,\ and\ -\/O2\ generates}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00154\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ a\ simple\ 8-\/byte\ copy\ loop.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00155\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ With\ gcc\ on\ ppc64le,\ all\ of\ the\ LZ4\_decompress\_*\ and\ LZ4\_wildCopy8}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00156\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ functions\ are\ annotated\ with\ \_\_attribute\_\_((optimize("{}O2"{}))),}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00157\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ and\ also\ LZ4\_wildCopy8\ is\ forcibly\ inlined,\ so\ that\ the\ O2\ attribute}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00158\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ of\ LZ4\_wildCopy8\ does\ not\ affect\ the\ compression\ speed.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00159\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00160\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if\ defined(\_\_PPC64\_\_)\ \&\&\ defined(\_\_LITTLE\_ENDIAN\_\_)\ \&\&\ defined(\_\_GNUC\_\_)\ \&\&\ !defined(\_\_clang\_\_)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00161\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#\ \ define\ LZ4\_FORCE\_O2\ \ \_\_attribute\_\_((optimize("{}O2"{})))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00162\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#\ \ undef\ LZ4\_FORCE\_INLINE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00163\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#\ \ define\ LZ4\_FORCE\_INLINE\ \ static\ \_\_inline\ \_\_attribute\_\_((optimize("{}O2"{}),always\_inline))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00164\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00165\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#\ \ define\ LZ4\_FORCE\_O2}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00166\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00167\ }

\DoxyCodeLine{00214\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ and\ be\ available\ at\ link\ time\ */}}
